<userid>100410394892811316463< /userid>< Text>
Ill start by saying I dont trust many shops around here with my car. After an incident on the highway that left my bumper, hood, grille, and fenders damaged, I decided to take my Mitsubishi Evo X to caliber to get the work done. They listened to my requests about the repair as well as took good care of my car while it was at the shop. There was constant communication and I was even emailed pictures to make sure the parts ordered were the correct parts. Three days later my car was done. After looking over the car I can say they painted and repaired the front of my car like new and I would recommend them to anyone... especially car guys like myself who wont take anything less than 100%. My Evo looks new again and I want to thank Carlos the manager and the rest of the team that worked on my car. 5 stars and my new trusted shop for any body work I need.<//Text>

< Review>
An absolutely stellar, true and original Butcher Shop. It's an, at least, monthly stop for a healthy Ribeye and marrow bones for the puppy. Sure, the meat is slightly more expensive than the other two grocery stores in town. Yet, the quality you get far exceeds that of the two grocery stores. And the selection available at the Butcher Shop is amazing.

And now that they have their Baskets (Essentials, Lean, Good for Grillin' and Smoking's a Good Habit), it's the only place locally that I am buying my meats. Matter of fact, just picked up the Lean Basket and substituting two items was done without hesitation.< /Review>

< review>
First off I would like to say that everyone I met at the center was very nice, (speakers and classmates). I took the 3 hour class where the speaker lectured to the students in regards to how to make money in the stock futures and options market. During the speech, I was called into a private room and was given a pressure sales pitch to purchase classes that was very expensive. I told the sales person that I could not afford them. The sales person said,  "let me see if you qualify for a loan." When the sales person came back, "I was told you are all set if you can come up with a specific amount." After speaking with other students in my 3 hour class, I found they got the same sales pitch and qualified for the same loan amount. I took the class twice at the center and took careful notes each time and I have also taken lots of the online classes XLT. I even tried using pro picks (the ticker symbols recommended daily by OTA for trading). Only to find out that the majority of trades stop out for a lost. The strategy does not work and to make matters even worse the center that I paid to attend in my area has shut down. The students that I have spoken with in my area have had the same experience. Please see attachment.Posted by Floyd H.< /review>

< review>
Update 9/2/20. After my original review was posted, I received a call from Chris Crum, the owner of OTA KC. His voicemail said wanted to discuss my "request for a refund". I responded in writing, stating we needed written communication for both of our interest. No response after 3 weeks. Also, they disabled reviews on their Facebook page so that my review could not be seen there.

As a "Mastermind Student" (top package), I am 100% DISSATISFIED with OTA OF KC, and my "investment" into OTA has been a complete waste of time and money.
1. OTA OF KC Misrepresented the Time Investment Required
2. OTA OF KC Misrepresented Projected Income
3. OTA CORPORATE'S Training "Product" Contains Significant Amount of Conflicts in Training Instruction

1. OTA OF KC frequently cited the following before purchase: "You can set your trades and forget it. You only need a couple of hours each day. Trade anytime day or night. Most students are profitable within six months." The realities are that time investment required is substantial, and OTA trainers refuted these claims in more advanced classes from other areas that stated:
"Setting your trades and not monitoring them is a high risk for loss and not advised. Setting your trades at night and letting them run is foolish. It takes years, many hours of training, and tons of hard work to become a profitable trader. Technically you can place a trade any time of day, but doing so outside of the peak hours of 7 AM to 11 AM M-F is foolish." The few successful traders I have spoken to all have stated that it took 3-5 years to become profitable, after spending 20+ hours each week.  None of my OTA fellow students I have kept in touch with have become profitable after 20 months and substantial time investment. OTA OF KC had foreknowledge about my schedule limitations, yet never provided caution of time needed. Repeatedly, they assured me of flexibility and minimal time investment.

2. OTA OF KC projected income thru a customized "trade plan". Goals, objectives, and projections were all provided by OTA OF KC, based on their calculations. As described above, Schedule limitations were NOT taken into account when accessing "trading risks" within their plan. OTA OF KC failed to disclose "No Entry Trades" during income projections, success rates, or training. OTA's own student accessible "MYOTA" website shows their "Pro Picks" professional trade recommendations from December 27, 2018, till May 27, 2020, are as follows::
558 recommended trades
35 Closed for Break Even
50 Closed for Loss
59 Closed for Profit
414 never made an entry (74%)
No entry trades use margin and limit the number of trades you can place per day, thereby affecting your profitability. Despite "no entry trades," accounting for over 74%, OTA OF KC failed to disclose "no entries" during training, trade plan creation or projected income. This information is not common knowledge by a novice trader. When I asked for help, OTA OF KC and OTA corporate said to "watch more videos".

3. Training materials are not taught consistently between instructors, which causes SIGNIFICANT confusion to students. It is unnecessarily frustrating and leads to students' poor trading results. This problem is common knowledge among OTA staff and trainers.  Drastic and vast differences in training methods require an immeasurable amount of time for a new student to determine correctly. Making OTA's "training product" a disputable "benefit" over other far less expensive trading classes.

All items stated in this review are verifiable. A simple google search into FTC suit against OTA validates these statements and confirms OTA's long-standing practice of buying off bad reviews.

When I requested a refund, they denied it. OTA OF KC cited a three-day clause for "returns". No product this complex or this expensive is possible within that short time-frame. OTA OF KC never saught to resolve my complaints, provide solutions, or even apologize despite spending $48k with their organization. A huge regret that I hope others avoid.<//review>

< Review>
On 08/17/2018 I wrote :
For beginners, I am not associated with OTA (Online Trading Academy), nor its administration, and I am not providing this review as part of a promotional reimbursement.
My experience with OTA, its staff and instructors, has been very positive, even though I have taken classes for only two months.
My motivation for selecting OTA to lead me through the myriad paths of investing in the financial markets is multi-faceted :
1) I have a desire to proactively control how my hard-earned money is used for my retirement.
2) I have a desire to alter my old career paths into a more rewarding, and more profitable direction.
3) I need help understanding how to apply the financial resources available to me to achieve my goals.
4) I want professional, experienced, and enthusiastic guidance for embarking on my new career path, and to support me down the road when I need it.
5) I want results sooner, not later, to allow me the time to enjoy the results of my effort.
Guess what ?  OTA meets all of my requirements.  After researching my many possibilities for the best method of reaching my goals, I decided on OTA.  From the sales personnel, to the educational counselors, instructors, support staff, and administrative personnel, all the way down to the actual campus facility and its accommodations, there was never a doubt that I made the right decision.
Attending the OTA training is like going back to college to learn a new profession.  Sure it is hard work, time-consuming, and not inexpensive.  But that means that achieving my goals will be worth every investment I make - professionally and financially.  To the reviewers who complain about the cost of this education, I would ask that if you value the quality of your training, at what price would you "book your order to buy" ?  And the parallel to the old adage that "you get what you pay for", is that "you DON'T get what you DON'T pay for".
My appreciation goes to all OTA personnel, and especially my instructors - Steve Hanahoe (Core Strategy), Tim Blotzer (Options), and Jerry Baldwin (Futures), and my education counselor Andy Dominguez.
One of my favorite pieces of advice from the OTA crew is "What you do now will secure your financial success for the rest of your life" - words I intend to live by.<//Review>

< text>
I first attended OTA as a newbie in August and over the first three days was floored by the mass of knowledge nestled in the folds of Irvine's metropolis- knowledge that many if not all of my peers knew nothing of. I was back again in September for the ProTrader class and once again  was impressed by the professional expertise of the instructors and staff, but also the down to earth amicability that warms the otherwise A/Ced building.

Every instructor is different- they all have different styles of teaching and trading and they respect that each and every student is an individual with their own mind and their own 'Why'.
OTA gets five stars in my reckoning because in the collective 15 days I've spent in classes their, I've learned about as much in a full semester of *normal* school; for those of you that know Plato's allegory of the Cave, it's like that.<//text>

< review>
A fabulous hole in the wall place at the crossroads of Beach and Artesia. I've never had Colombian food before but it will not be the last. Having ordered the Bandeja Paisa which was a mountain of meat on a bed of white rice, a side of the best beans ever, a sunny side egg, and half an avocado, the chicharron was fried to perfection and by far my favorite. Though it took 30 minutes for my food, it was well worth the wait. The server was kind and considerate.<//review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Great ambience with lots of flat screen TVs everywhere and lots of outdoor seating too! Happy Hour until 7pm. Good food and good service. Just note that two thirds of the indoors is designated as bar seating with high top tables, yet only the bar counter itself is first come first serve seating. The high top tables require you to put your name down and wait. The chicken tacos are great. The fried mushrooms are great. The fried pickles are not that great because they're thick sliced and the breading is falling off. The Bourbon Honey Mustard is my favorite wing sauce.<//review>

< Text>
For the last 2 years every Thursday my wife and I go to Buffalo Wild Wings. We have our go to spots but also try new locations. This particular location is literally 2 blocks from our house, but we try to avoid it when we can. They are over staffed however still manage terrible and slow service. The food is always dry even after we say extra wet, and never consistent. Multiple times our mozzarella sticks have come out cold, the cheese inside is literally a block.

Twice we've been sat in dirty tables, I assumed after the waiter took our drink order they would come back to clean it. Thank corporate for providing those wet wipes, which I used to clean the table.

If you do come to this locations ask to sit in Bills section, best server there.

I'll take a trip here just to take pictures of the food, I'll edit my post with the images soon.</Text>
